 // 猜你喜欢
 function handleGuess() {
 var BASE_INTF = '//price.pcauto.com.cn/price/api/v1/serialgroup/user_like_recommend_group?uid={uid}&rid=3&encode=gbk&callback=showGuessCon'; // 车型库出基础车系数据
 var sids = '';
 var key = 'pcauto_guess_group';
 var useStorage = window.localStorage && window.JSON;
 // 内容
 window.showGuessCon = function(data, fromStorage) {
 var dataArr = data;
 if(dataArr.length == 0){
 showGroup();
 return;
 }
 document.body.insertBefore(document.createElement("script"),document.body.firstChild).src = "//count.pcauto.com.cn/count.php?channel=808&screen="+screen.width+"*"+screen.height+"&refer="+encodeURIComponent(document.referrer)+"&anticache="+new Date().getTime()+"&url="+encodeURIComponent(location.href)+"&from=event";
 common.$$("j-pcauto-cooperation").style.display='block';
 var html = '', sidStr = '',cStr,priceStr,str1,price,count;
 for (var i = 0; i < dataArr.length && i < 5; i++) {
 var item = dataArr[i],price;
 sidStr += (!sidStr? '' : ',') + item.id;
 if (0 == i) {
 cStr = 'fir';
 }else{
 cStr = '';
 }
 price=item.price
 if(price.indexOf("万")){
 priceStr='<a href="//price.pcauto.com.cn/sg' + item.id + '/market/r3/#ad=11806" target="_blank">' + price + '</a>'
 }else{
 priceStr=price;
 }
 var count=item.discountPrice.maxDiscount;
 if(count!=0){
 str1='<i class="discount">降'+ count +'万<i class="iconTri"></i></i>';
 }else{
 str1='';
 }
 html +='<div class="pic-txt-auto '+cStr+' ">'+
 '<a target="_blank" href="//price.pcauto.com.cn/sg' + item.id + '/#ad=11806" class="pic">'+
 '<img src="' + item.photo + '" alt="" width="204" height="153" />'+
 '</a>'+
 '<p class="subTit"><span class="tit"><a target="_blank" href="//price.pcauto.com.cn/sg' + item.id + '/#ad=11806">' + item.name + '</a></span>'+
 '<span class="price">' + priceStr +'</span></p>'+
 '<div class="tip">'+
 '<a target="_blank" href="//price.pcauto.com.cn/dealer/commorders/order.jsp?t=0&sgid=' + item.id + '#ad=11806" class="fir">询底价</a><a target="_blank" href="//jr.pcauto.com.cn/autofinance/commorders/order.jsp?sgid=' + item.id + '#ad=11806">分期购车</a><a target="_blank" href="//price.pcauto.com.cn/dealer/commorders/order.jsp?t=4&sgid=' + item.id + '#ad=11806">置换</a>'+
 '</div>'+str1+'</div>'
 }
 var guessWrapElm = document.getElementById('JslideWrapGuess');
 if (!html || !guessWrapElm) return;
 guessWrapElm.innerHTML = html;
 if (useStorage && !fromStorage) {
 // 保存数据到 localStorage
 dataArr.push(+new Date + 30 * 60 * 1000); // 记录有效时间至30min后
 localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(dataArr));
 }
 };
 // 初始化
 function initGuess() {
 var uValue = common.getCookie('u');
 if (!uValue) {showGroup();return};
 var value = useStorage && localStorage.getItem(key);
 var data = value && JSON.parse(value);
 var time = data && data.length > 1 && data.pop() || 0;
 if (+new Date > time) {
 common.getScript(BASE_INTF.replace('{uid}', uValue));
 } else {
 showGuessCon(data, true);
 }
 };
 initGuess();
 }

 function BatchUploader(flvUrl, thumb, id, isPlay) {

 BatchUploader.prototype.show = function() {
 var flashVars = "useExternalInterface=Yes&volume=" + encodeURIComponent(this.volume)
 //+ "&process=" + encodeURIComponent(this.process) 
 + "&domain=" + encodeURIComponent(this.domain) + "&flv=" + encodeURIComponent(this.flv) + "&thumb=" + encodeURIComponent(this.thumb) + "&id=" + encodeURIComponent(this.id) + "&autoplay=" + encodeURIComponent(this.autoplay)
 + "&onevent=" + encodeURIComponent(this.onevent)
 + "&skin=" + encodeURIComponent(this.skin) + "&pt=" + encodeURIComponent(this.pt) + "&loadswf=" + encodeURIComponent(this.loadswf) + "&controlbar=" + encodeURIComponent(this.controlbar) + "&pointUrl=" + encodeURIComponent(this.pointUrl)
 //+"&albumid=" + encodeURIComponent(this.albumid)
 //+"&currentid=" + encodeURIComponent(this.currentid)
 + "&onplaycallback=" + encodeURIComponent(this.onplaycallback) + "&onpausecallback=" + encodeURIComponent(this.onpausecallback) + "&onresumecallback=" + encodeURIComponent(this.onresumecallback) + "&onendcallback=" + encodeURIComponent(this.onendcallback)
 //  +"&adh=" + encodeURIComponent(this.adh)
 //  + "&adm=" + encodeURIComponent(this.adm)
 //  +"&adhtime=" + encodeURIComponent(this.adhtime)
 ;
 var str = '';
 str += '<object id="pcplayer" style="background:#000;" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=9,0,115" height="456" width="798">' +
 '<param name="movie" value="'+this.flashUrl+'">' +
 '<param name="allowScriptAccess" value="always">' +
 '<param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">' +
 '<param name="menu" value="false">' +
 '<param name="flashvars" value="'+flashVars+'">' +
 '<param value="window" name="wmode">' +
 '<embed name="pcplayer" style="background:#000;" src="'+this.flashUrl+'" flashvars="'+flashVars+'" wmode="window" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" height="456" width="798" allowScriptAccess="always" allowFullScreen="true" menu="false" pluginspage="http://www.macromedia.com/go/getflashplayer">' +
 '</object>';
 return str;
 }
 window.onplaycallback=function() {
 var first=$("#switch-e-1").attr("data-init");
 if(first!=1){
 var id,oNum,iNum;
 $("#switch-e-1").attr("data-init",1);
 o=$(".switch-e-con .tab").eq(0)
 id=o.attr("data-id");
 oNum=$(".id"+id);
 iNum=parseInt(oNum.html());
 common.getScript("//pchouse.pcvideo.com.cn/__counter.jsp?video="+id);
 oNum.html(iNum+1);
 }
 setText("播放中");
 }
 window.onpausecallback=function() {
 setText("暂停");
 }
 window.onresumecallback=function() {
 setText("播放中");
 }
 window.setText=function(str){
 var index=$("#switch-e-1").attr("data-index"),o=$("#switch-e-1 .switch-e-box").eq(index),subIndex=o.attr("data-play");
 o.find(".overlay").eq(subIndex).html(str);
 }
 window.onendcallback=function() {
 document.pcplayer.resume();
 document.pcplayer.seek(0);
 var index=$("#switch-e-1").attr("data-index"),o=$("#switch-e-1 .switch-e-box").eq(index),subIndex=o.attr("data-play"),nextIndex;
 if(subIndex==4){
 nextIndex=0;
 }else{
 nextIndex=parseInt(subIndex)+1;
 }
 palyVideo(index,nextIndex,true,1);
 var eTab=o.find(".tab"),eBox=$("#switch-e-1 .video");
 eTab.eq(subIndex).find(".overlay").html("").hide();
 eTab.eq(nextIndex).find(".overlay").html("播放中").show();
 var numO=$(".id"+eTab.eq(nextIndex).attr("data-id")),numI=parseInt(numO.html());
 numO.html(numI+1);
 o.attr("data-play",nextIndex);
 }
 function palyVideo(index,playIndex,isPlay){
 var eTab=$(".switch-e-con .tab"),eBox=$("#switch-e-1 .switch-e-box"),curTab=eBox.eq(index).find(".tab").eq(playIndex);
 var flvUrl = curTab.attr("data-flvUrl"),
 thumb = curTab.attr("data-thumb"),
 id=curTab.attr("data-id");
 var lotteryloader = new BatchUploader(flvUrl, thumb, id, isPlay),
 str = lotteryloader.show();
 $("#switch-e-1 .video").html(str);
 if(isPlay==true){
 common.getScript("//pchouse.pcvideo.com.cn/__counter.jsp?video="+id);
 }
 }
 palyVideo(0,0,false);
 $(".switch-e-box .tab").each(function(i,el){
 $(el).bind('click', function() {
 var index=$(".switch-e-tab .current").prevAll().length,cur=i%5,str=$(el).find(".overlay").html(),first=$("#switch-e-1").attr("data-init");
 if(first!=1){
 $("#switch-e-1").attr("data-init",1);
 }
 if(str=="播放中"){return;}
 var numO=$(".id"+$(this).attr("data-id")),numI=parseInt(numO.html());
 numO.html(numI+1);
 palyVideo(index,cur,true,1);
 $("#switch-e-1 .overlay").html("").hide();
 $(el).find(".overlay").html("播放中").show();
 $(el).parents(".switch-e-box").attr("data-play",cur);
 $("#switch-e-1").attr("data-index",index)
 })
 })
